add_namespace = rcmjapan
# Chinese Refuse Concessions
country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.1
	title = rcmjapan.1.t
	desc = rcmjapan.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_01

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rcmjapan.1.a
	}

}

# Chinese Concessions
country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.2
	title = rcmjapan.2.t
	desc = rcmjapan.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_running

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rcmjapan.2.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = hpc_pro_jap }
				news_event = { days = 15 id = news.1302 }
			}
			news_event = { days = 5 id = news.1 }
		}
		JAP = {
			give_guarantee = HPC
		}
	}

}

# Soviets Push Back And Win
country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.3
	title = rcmjapan.3.t
	desc = rcmjapan.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_soviet_soldiers_tank

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
			761 = {
				is_owned_by = JAP
				any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = SOV } }
			}
			761 = { add_manpower = -30000 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					761 = {
						is_owned_by = JAP
						any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = SOV }
					}
				}
			}
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = { any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = SOV } }
				add_manpower = -30000
			}
		}

		army_experience = 5
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = rcmjapan.3.t #test_the_ussr_focus
			bonus = 0.5
			uses = 1
			category = cat_anti_tank
		}
		name = rcmjapan.3.a
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = soviet.2 }
		}
	}
}
# Soviets Push Back And Lose
country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.4
	title = rcmjapan.4.t
	desc = rcmjapan.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_japanese_soldiers_01

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rcmjapan.4.a
		if = {
			limit = {
			761 = {
				is_owned_by = JAP
				any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = SOV } }
			}
			761 = { add_manpower = -20000 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					761 = {
						is_owned_by = JAP
						any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = SOV }
					}
				}
			}
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = { any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = SOV } }
				add_manpower = -20000
			}
		}
		army_experience = 15
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = rcmjapan.4.t #test_the_ussr_focus
			bonus = 0.5
			uses = 1
			category = cat_grand_battle_plan
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = soviet.3 }
		}
	}
}

# Siam event from Japan: Become puppet or not
country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.12
	title = rcmjapan.12.t
	desc = rcmjapan.12.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_japanese_officers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rcmjapan.12.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100#GUO
		}
		JAP = {
			country_event = { id = rcmjapan.13 }
			effect_tooltip = { add_to_faction = SIA }#GUO
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rcmjapan.12.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }#GUO
		JAP = {
			country_event = { id = rcmjapan.14 }
			effect_tooltip = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = SIA
					type = puppet_wargoal_focus
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rcmjapan.15.a
		hidden_effect = {
			load_oob = "JAP_Indian_National_Army_reinforcement"
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = JAP_Indian_National_Army_arrives
		add_manpower = 10000
		set_global_flag = indian_national_army_setup
		RAJ = {
			add_stability = -0.2
			add_ideas = RAJ_azad_hind
		}
		ENG = {
			country_event = { id = britain.19 }
		}
	}
}

#country_event = {
#	id = rcmjapan.22

country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.27
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		has_completed_focus = JAP_intervene_in_china
		is_subject_of = JAP
		OR = {
			tag = HPC
			tag = EHB
			tag = RFM
		}
		has_country_flag = im_rrc_now
		CHI = { is_puppet_of = JAP }
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			annex_country = { target = CHI transfer_troops = yes }
			annex_country = { target = RFM transfer_troops = yes }
			annex_country = { target = EHB transfer_troops = yes }
			if = {
				limit = {
					HPC = {
						is_subject_of = JAP
						has_country_flag = im_rrc_now
					}
				}
				annex_country = { target = HPC transfer_troops = yes }
			}
			set_political_party = { ideology = neutrality popularity = 55 }
			set_political_party = { ideology = fascism popularity = 45 }
			set_politics = { ruling_party = neutrality elections_allowed = no }
			RRC_core = yes
			JAP = { puppet = ROOT }
		}
	}
	option = {}
}

country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.30
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		exists = yes
		has_country_flag = im_jnc_now
		has_global_flag = jnc_exists
		OR = {
			RFM = { has_full_control_of_state = 597 }
			RFM = { has_full_control_of_state = 1028 }
			RFM = { has_full_control_of_state = 743 }
			RFM = { has_full_control_of_state = 614 }
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					RFM = { has_full_control_of_state = 597 }
				}
				set_state_controller = 597
			    set_state_owner = 597 ###
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					RFM = { has_full_control_of_state = 1028 }
				}
				set_state_controller = 1028
			    set_state_owner = 597 ###
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					RFM = { has_full_control_of_state = 743 }
				}
				set_state_controller = 743
			    set_state_owner = 743 ###
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					RFM = { has_full_control_of_state = 614 }
				}
				set_state_controller = 614
			    set_state_owner = 614 ###
			}
		}
	}
	option = {}
}
country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.31
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		exists = yes
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = im_rrc_now
				tag = EHB
				597 = { is_owned_by = EHB }
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = im_rrc_now
				tag = HPC
				597 = { is_owned_by = HPC }
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = im_rrc_now
				tag = RFM
				597 = { is_owned_by = RFM }
			}
		}
		JAP = {
			has_full_control_of_state = 608
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_state_controller = 608
		}
	}
	option = {}
}

#embargo japan? (britian)
country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.9321
	title = rcmjapan.9321.t
	desc = rcmjapan.9321.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_japanese_soldiers_03
	immediate = {
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan.9321.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = embargo }
		set_global_flag = abcd_b
		USA = {
			country_event = { #days = 1
				id = rcmjapan.93211
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { RAJ = { is_subject_of = ENG } }
			RAJ = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = embargo } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { MAL = { is_subject_of = ENG } }
			MAL = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = embargo } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { SST = { is_subject_of = ENG } }
			SST = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = embargo } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { BOR = { is_subject_of = ENG } }
			BOR = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = embargo } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { BUR = { is_subject_of = ENG } }
			BUR = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = embargo } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { SAR = { is_subject_of = ENG } }
			SAR = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = embargo } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { CAN = { is_subject_of = ENG } }
			CAN = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = embargo } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { AST = { is_subject_of = ENG } }
			AST = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = embargo } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { SAF = { is_subject_of = ENG } }
			SAF = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = embargo } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan.9321.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		USA = {
			country_event = { #days = 1
				id = rcmjapan.93212
			}
		}
	}
}

#puppet transfer states<=JAP/not the right ruler
country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.33
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		exists = yes
		OR = {
			JAP = {
				has_completed_focus = JAP_intervene_in_china
			}
			date > 1939.1.1
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {#tag = EHB
				tag = EHB
				has_global_flag = jnc_exists
			}
			AND = {#tag = hpc
				tag = HPC
				is_subject_of = JAP
			}
			tag = RFM
			tag = ECA
		}
		is_puppet_of = JAP
		NOT = { has_country_flag = transfer_state_loop }
		num_of_controlled_states > 1
		any_other_country = {
			has_war_with = ROOT
			has_war_with = JAP
			OR = {
				is_originally_warlord = yes
				is_legit_china = yes
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	immediate = {
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = ROOT.core_states
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
						is_fully_controlled_by = JAP
						controller = {
							is_subject_of = JAP
							has_full_control_of_state = PREV
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						is_owned_by = ECA
					}
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
				ROOT = { set_state_controller = PREV }
			}
		}
		country_event = { hours = 8 id = rcmjapan.9834 }
	}
	option = {
		set_country_flag = transfer_state_loop
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.9834
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = transfer_state_loop
	}
	option = {
	}
}

#puppet transfer states#CHI #change to on action
country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.634
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = transfer_state_loop_chi
		FROM = {
			country_event = { days = 1 id = rcmjapan.633 }
		}
	}
	option = {
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.633
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			is_legit_china = yes
			is_warlord = yes
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = transfer_state_loop_chi }
		has_war_with = JAP
		any_neighbor_country = {
			has_war_with = ROOT
		}
		any_of_scopes = {				
			array = global.small_china
			tooltip = small_china_tt
			ROOT = {
				has_full_control_of_state = PREV
				NOT = {
					owns_state = PREV
				}
			}
			owner = {
				has_war_with = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	immediate = {
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.small_china
			tooltip = small_china_tt
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						has_full_control_of_state = PREV
						NOT = {
							owns_state = PREV
						}
					}
					owner = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
					NOT = {
						is_capital_of_japan_puppet = yes
					}
				}
				#if = {#NO COMMIE MILITIA #this is changed to use on actions
				#	limit = {
				#		NOT = { has_state_flag = commie_ridden_states }
				#		NOT = { has_state_flag = commie_amassed_support } #now they gotta amass support before they can take over it directly
				#	}
				#	add_core_of = ROOT
				#	ROOT = { set_state_owner = PREV }
				#}
				######COMMUNIST TAKE OVER
				if = {#COMMIE MILITIA AMASSED SUPPORT
					limit = {
						#has_state_flag = commie_amassed_support
						is_core_of = event_target:WTT_communist_china
						has_state_flag = commie_ridden_states
					}
					event_target:WTT_communist_china = { transfer_state = PREV }
					clr_state_flag = commie_ridden_states
				}
			}
		}
		country_event = { days = 1 id = rcmjapan.634 }
		set_country_flag = transfer_state_loop_chi
	}
	option = {
	}

country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.636
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		exists = yes
		OR = {
			JAP = {
				has_completed_focus = JAP_intervene_in_china
			}
			date > 1939.1.1
		}
		AND = {
			OR = {
				country_exists = RFM
				country_exists = EHB
				AND = {
					country_exists = HPC
					HPC = {
						is_subject_of = JAP
					}
				}
				has_global_flag = jnc_exists
			}
			tag = JAP
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = transfer_state_loop_jap }
		num_of_controlled_states > 1
		has_war_with = CHI
		NOT = {
			any_of_scopes = {
				array = JAP.subjects
				is_rrc = yes
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	immediate = {
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.big_china
			if = {
				limit = {
					controller = {
						is_subject_of = JAP
						has_full_control_of_state = PREV
					}
					NOT = {
						any_of_scopes = {
							array = JAP.subjects
							PREV = {
								OR = {
									is_claimed_by = PREV
									is_core_of = PREV
								}
							}
						}
					}
					owner = {
						has_war_with = JAP
					}
				}
				JAP = { set_state_controller = PREV }
			}
		}
		country_event = { days = 1 id = rcmjapan.635 }
	}
	option = {
		set_country_flag = transfer_state_loop_jap
	}
}
#Expand RRC#
country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.34
	title = rcmjapan.34.t
	desc = rcmjapan.34.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_japanese_handshake
	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		NOT = { country_exists = CHI }
		NOT = {
			any_enemy_country = {
				exists = yes
				OR = {
					is_warlord = yes
					TAG = PRC
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				EHB = { has_country_flag = im_rrc_now }
				country_exists = EHB
				EHB = { is_neighbor_of = JAP }
			}
			AND = {
				HPC = { is_subject_of = JAP }
				HPC = { has_country_flag = im_rrc_now }
				country_exists = HPC
				HPC = { is_neighbor_of = JAP }
			}
			AND = {
				RFM = { has_country_flag = im_rrc_now }
				country_exists = RFM
				RFM = { is_neighbor_of = JAP }
			}
			AND = {
				621 = {
				   is_owned_by = JAP
				   is_core_of = ECA
			    }
				746 = {
				   is_owned_by = JAP
				   is_core_of = ECA
			    }
				1019 = {
					is_owned_by = JAP
					is_core_of = ECA
				}
				1020 = {
					is_owned_by = JAP
					is_core_of = ECA
				}
			}
		}
		any_owned_state = {
			OR = {
				is_core_of = EHB
				is_core_of = RFM
				is_core_of = ECA
				is_claimed_by = EHB
				is_claimed_by = RFM
				is_claimed_by = ECA
				AND = {
					is_core_of = HPC
					HPC = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				AND = {
					is_claimed_by = HPC
					HPC = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}		
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RRC_expand }
		AND = {
			NOT = {
				any_other_country = {
					OR = {
						is_warlord = yes
						TAG = PRC
					}
					OR = {
						JAP = {
							has_wargoal_against = PREV
						}
						JAP = {
							has_war_with = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = RRC_expand
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan.34.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		add_stability = 0.1
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_of_scopes = {
						array = JAP.subjects
						is_rrc = yes
					}
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_controlled_by = JAP
					OR = {
						is_core_of = EHB
						is_claimed_by = EHB
					}
					NOT = {
						HPC = {
							is_subject_of = JAP
						}
					}
				}
				EHB = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_controlled_by = JAP
					HPC = {
						is_subject_of = JAP
					}
					EHB = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = im_jnc_now
						}
					}
					OR = {
						is_core_of = HPC
						is_claimed_by = HPC
					}
				}
				HPC = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_controlled_by = JAP
					OR = {
						is_core_of = RFM
						is_claimed_by = RFM
					}
				}
				RFM = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				EHB = { has_country_flag = im_rrc_now }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_controlled_by = JAP
					OR = {
						is_core_of = EHB
						is_claimed_by = EHB
					}
				}
				EHB = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				HPC = { has_country_flag = im_rrc_now }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_controlled_by = JAP
					OR = {
						is_core_of = HPC
						is_claimed_by = HPC
					}
				}
				HPC = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			else = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_controlled_by = JAP
						OR = {
							is_core_of = RFM
							is_claimed_by = RFM
						}
					}
					RFM = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_controlled_by = JAP
				OR = {
					is_core_of = ECA
					is_claimed_by = ECA
				}
			}
			ECA = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		country_event = { hours = 3 id = rcmjapan.535 }
		#ECA = { country_event = { hours = 3 id = rcmjapan.736 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan.34.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		add_stability = -0.1
		country_event = { hours = 3 id = rcmjapan.535 }
	}
}

							option = OKADA_STAYS_TREATY_FACTION
						}

							rule = JAP_ai_behavior
							option = OKADA_STAYS_STATE_SOCIALISM
						}

							option = OKADA_STAYS_COMMUNISM
						}

							option = OKADA_STAYS_TOHOKAI
						}
					}
				}
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		hidden_effect ={
			set_global_flag = kodoha_failed
			set_global_flag = okada_stays
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			add_idea = JAP_kodoha_plot_2

		}

#emperor's mind
country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.47
	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		NOT = { has_completed_focus = showa_restoration_focus }
		focus_progress = {
			focus = showa_restoration_focus
			progress > 0.2
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		#if = {
		#	limit = {
		#		OR = {
		#			is_historical_focus_on = yes
		#			AND = {
		#				has_country_flag = genro_purged_by_kodoha
		#				has_country_flag = prince_purged_by_kodoha
		#			}
		#		}
		#	}
		#	set_country_flag = emperor_refuses
		#}
		if = {
			limit = {
				#NOT = { is_historical_focus_on = yes }
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = genro_purged_by_kodoha
					has_country_flag = prince_purged_by_kodoha
				}
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = genro_purged_by_kodoha
						has_country_flag = prince_purged_by_kodoha
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_idea = saionji_kinmochi
						has_idea = kanin_kotohito
					}
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				75 = { set_country_flag = emperor_refuses }
				25 = { set_global_flag = nothing_here }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				#NOT = { is_historical_focus_on = yes }
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = genro_purged_by_kodoha
					has_country_flag = prince_purged_by_kodoha
				}
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = genro_purged_by_kodoha
						has_country_flag = prince_purged_by_kodoha
					}
				}
				OR = {
					has_idea = saionji_kinmochi
					has_idea = kanin_kotohito
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				50 = { set_country_flag = emperor_refuses }
				50 = { set_global_flag = nothing_here }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				#NOT = { is_historical_focus_on = yes }
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = genro_purged_by_kodoha
						has_country_flag = prince_purged_by_kodoha
					}
				}
				OR = {
					has_idea = saionji_kinmochi
					has_idea = kanin_kotohito
				}
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						has_idea = saionji_kinmochi
						has_idea = kanin_kotohito
					}
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				30 = { set_country_flag = emperor_refuses }
				70 = { set_global_flag = nothing_here }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				#NOT = { is_historical_focus_on = yes }
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = genro_purged_by_kodoha
						has_country_flag = prince_purged_by_kodoha
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_idea = saionji_kinmochi
					has_idea = kanin_kotohito
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				0 = { set_country_flag = emperor_refuses }
				100 = { set_global_flag = nothing_here }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
	}
}

				}

				}
				if = {
					limit = { JAP = { NOT = {  has_completed_focus = JAP_expand_the_revolutions_focus } } }

				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { hours = 5 id = rcmjapan.69 }
		}
	}
}

#the creation of MEN (ACCEPT, 1st time)
country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.984
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { #so china and SHX get to keep what they captured
			if = {
				limit = {
					PLM = {
						OR = {
							has_war_with = CHI
							has_war_with = SHX
						}						
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							PLM = {
								controls_state = 1014
							}
						}
					}
					SHX = {
						transfer_state = 1014
						transfer_state = 621
						transfer_state = 746
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							PLM = {
								AND = { 
									controls_state = 621
								    controls_state = 746 
							    }
							}
						}
					}
					SHX = {
						transfer_state = 621
						transfer_state = 746
					}
				}			
			}
		}
		PLM = {
			every_unit_leader = {
			    set_nationality = ROOT
			}
		}
		annex_country = {
			target = PLM
			transfer_troops = yes
		}
		MEN_CREATION = yes
	}
	option = {
	}
}

	title = rcmjapan.89.t
	desc = rcmjapan.89.d

			has_global_flag = de_is_in_charge
		}

		has_global_flag = mua_exists
		date > 1938.3.18
		date < 1939.3.18
	}

		name = rcmjapan.89.a
		hidden_effect = {
			kill_country_leader = yes
			retire_country_leader = yes

				limit = {
					has_character = PLM_prince_demchugdongrub
				}
				PLM_prince_demchugdongrub = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							expire = "1965.1.1"
							ideology = fascism_ideology
							traits = {
							}
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}  
					add_country_leader_trait = spirit_of_genghis
				}
				else = {
					create_country_leader = {
					    name = "PLM_prince_demchugdongrub"
						desc = "POLITICS_DEMCHUGDONGRUB_DESC"
						picture = "gfx/leaders/MEN/Portrait_MEN_Demchugdongrub.dds"
						expire = "1966.4.23"
						ideology = fascism_ideology
						traits = {
							spirit_of_genghis
						}
				    }
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = de_is_in_charge
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = Demchugdongrub_new_leader
	}
}

#MAN rebuild #MAN
country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.1002
	title = rcmjapan.1002.t
	desc = rcmjapan.1002.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_MAN_official

	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		is_subject = no
		328 = {
			is_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = yes
			#is_owned_by = JAP
		}
		NOT = {
			country_exists = MAN
		}
		NOT = {#I don't want event pops-up
			has_country_flag = no_rebuild_MAN
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = MAN_no_more
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	option = {#YES
		name = rcmjapan.1002.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		MAN = {
			transfer_state = 328
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_manchuria_state = yes
				}
				add_core_of = MAN
			}
			army_experience = 25
			puppet_reclaim_land = yes
		}
		puppet = MAN
		hidden_effect = {
			MAN = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = fascism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				set_political_party = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = 30
				}
				set_political_party = {
					ideology = n_socialism
					popularity = 0
				}
				set_political_party = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = 0
				}
				set_political_party = {
					ideology = fascism
					popularity = 70
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_war_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
				}
				MAN = {
					event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {
						PREV = {
							add_to_war = {
								targeted_alliance = JAP
								enemy = PREV
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	#option = {#NO
	#	name = rcmjapan.1002.b
	#}
	option = {#NO FOREVER
		name = rcmjapan.1002.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = no_rebuild_MAN
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.1005
	title = rcmjapan.1005.t
	desc = rcmjapan.1005.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_new_reorganized_national_government

	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		is_subject = no
		OR = {
			1015 = {
				is_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = yes
				#is_owned_by = JAP
			}
			608 = {
				is_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = yes
				#is_owned_by = JAP
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			any_of_scopes = {
				array = ROOT.subjects
				exists = yes
				is_rrc = yes
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = no_rebuild_RRC
		}
		has_global_flag = rrc_exists
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	option = {#YES
		name = rcmjapan.1005.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = RRC_annex
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:RCM_RRC_puppet = {				
				if = {
					limit = {
						609 = { #east hebei
							is_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = yes
						}
					}
					609 = {
						PREV = { set_state_owner = PREV }
						set_state_province_controller = {
							controller = PREV
							limit = {
								OR = {
									is_ally_with = JAP
									tag = JAP
								}
							}
						}
					}
					#transfer_state = 609
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						613 = { #shanghai
							is_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = yes
						}
					}
					613 = {
						PREV = { set_state_owner = PREV }
						set_state_province_controller = {
							controller = PREV
							limit = {
								OR = {
									is_ally_with = JAP
									tag = JAP
								}
							}
						}
					}
					#transfer_state = 613
				}
				if = { #potential capital, transfer without full control
					limit = {
						1015 = {
							is_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = yes
							#is_owned_by = JAP
						}
					}					
					1015 = {
						PREV = { set_state_owner = PREV }
						set_state_province_controller = {
							controller = PREV
							limit = {
								OR = {
									is_ally_with = JAP
									tag = JAP
								}
							}
						}
					}
					#transfer_state = 1015
				}
				if = { #potential capital, transfer without full control
					limit = {
						608 = {
							is_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = yes
							#is_owned_by = JAP
						}
					}
					608 = {
						PREV = { set_state_owner = PREV }
						set_state_province_controller = {
							controller = PREV
							limit = {
								OR = {
									is_ally_with = JAP
									tag = JAP
								}
							}
						}
					}
					#transfer_state = 608
				}
				RRC_CREATION = yes
				get_current_government_type = yes
				JAP = {
					puppet = event_target:RCM_RRC_puppet
				}
				restore_previous_government_type = yes
				
			}
			event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {
				event_target:RCM_RRC_puppet = {
					add_to_war = {
						targeted_alliance = JAP
						enemy = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	#option = {#NO
	#	name = rcmjapan.1005.b
	#}
	option = {#NO FOREVER
		name = rcmjapan.1005.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		set_country_flag = no_rebuild_RRC
	}
}

			}

							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			ECA = {

					elections_allowed = no
				}
				set_political_party = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = 30
				}

					popularity = 0
				}

					ideology = communism
					popularity = 0
				}

					ideology = fascism
					popularity = 70
				}
			}
		}
	}

                delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Ch'iping Shih" } 
                delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Tuli Lü" }

			}

				}
			}

		}

			factor = 0

country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.1022
	title = rcmjapan.1022.t
	desc = rcmjapan.1022.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_new_reorganized_national_government
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = { #Give EHB to HPC
		name = rcmjapan.1022.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_ai = yes
				HPC = {
					is_ai = no
				}
			}
		}
		trigger =  {
			EHB = {
				is_puppet_of = ROOT
				OR = {
					is_ai = no
					CHI = {
						has_country_leader = { name = "None" ruling_only = yes }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		EHB = {	
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.small_china
				tooltip = small_china_tt
				add_core_of = PREV
			}
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.big_china
				tooltip = big_china_tt
				effect_tooltip = {
					add_claim_by = PREV
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { is_in_array = { global.small_china = This.id } }
					}
					add_claim_by = PREV
				}
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = EYW_jap_chi
			CHI = {
				get_current_government_type_global = yes
			}
			restore_previous_government_type_global = yes
			
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						CHI = { has_government = democratic }
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = CPG
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = democratic
						name = CHI_n_socialism_cdl
						long_name = CHI_n_socialism_cdl_long
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						CHI = { has_government = n_socialism }
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = CHI
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = n_socialism
						name = CHI_communism_party_POW
						long_name = CHI_communism_party_POW_long
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						CHI = { has_government = communism }
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = CHI_warlord_leader_communism
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = communism
						name = PRG_party
						long_name = PRG_party_long
					}
				}
			}
		}		
		CHI = { country_event = rcmjapan.1020 }
		HPC = { country_event = rcmjapan.1020 }
	}
	option = { #Give EHB to HPC
		name = rcmjapan.1022.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_ai = yes
				EHB = {
					is_ai = no
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_ai = yes
				CHI = {
					has_country_leader = { name = "None" ruling_only = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		trigger =  {
			HPC = {
				is_puppet_of = ROOT
				OR = {
					is_ai = no
					CHI = {
						has_country_leader = { name = "None" ruling_only = yes }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		HPC = {
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.small_china
				tooltip = small_china_tt
				add_core_of = PREV
			}
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.big_china
				tooltip = big_china_tt
				effect_tooltip = {
					add_claim_by = PREV
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { is_in_array = { global.small_china = This.id } }
					}
					add_claim_by = PREV
				}
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = EYW_jap_chi
			CHI = {
				get_current_government_type_global = yes
			}
			restore_previous_government_type_global = yes
			
						
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						CHI = { has_government = democratic }
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = CPG
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = democratic
						name = CHI_n_socialism_cdl
						long_name = CHI_n_socialism_cdl_long
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						CHI = { has_government = n_socialism }
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = CHI
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = n_socialism
						name = CHI_communism_party_POW
						long_name = CHI_communism_party_POW_long
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						CHI = { has_government = communism }
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = CHI_warlord_leader_communism
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = communism
						name = PRG_party
						long_name = PRG_party_long
					}
				}
			}
		}
		CHI = { country_event = rcmjapan.1021 }
		EHB = { country_event = rcmjapan.1021 }
	}
	option = { # Give EHB to China
		name = rcmjapan.1022.c
		trigger = { NOT = { CHI = { has_country_leader = { name = "None" ruling_only = yes } } } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				HPC = { is_puppet_of = ROOT is_ai = no }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				EHB = { is_puppet_of = ROOT is_ai = no }
			}
		}
		trigger =  { CHI = { is_puppet_of = ROOT } }
		CHI = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_government = communism
						has_government = n_socialism
					}	
				}
				load_focus_tree = warlord_generic_communist
			}
			else = {
				load_focus_tree = warlord_generic_nationalist
			}
		}
		HPC = { country_event = rcmjapan.1020 }
		EHB = { country_event = rcmjapan.1020 }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.90
	title = rcmjapan.90.t
	desc = rcmjapan.90.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_mengjiang_puppet_02

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {#BOTH EXIST
		name = rcmjapan.90.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			country_exists = NSG
			country_exists = SCG
		}
		SCG = {
			country_event = {
				hours = 1 id = rcmjapan.91
			}
		}
		NSG = {
			country_event = {
				hours = 5 id = rcmjapan.92
			}
		}
		create_mengjiang = yes
	}
	option = {#ONE EXIST
		name = rcmjapan.90.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				country_exists = NSG
				country_exists = SCG
			}
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					country_exists = NSG
					country_exists = SCG
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = SCG
			}
			transfer_state = 1013
			create_mengjiang = yes
			SCG = {
				country_event = {
					hours = 1 id = rcmjapan.91
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = NSG
			}
			transfer_state = 611
			create_mengjiang = yes
			NSG = {
				country_event = {
					hours = 5 id = rcmjapan.92
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {#NONE EXIST
		name = rcmjapan.90.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					country_exists = NSG
					country_exists = SCG
				}
			}
		}
		transfer_state = 1013
		transfer_state = 611
		create_mengjiang = yes
	}
}

		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = NSG_yes_mengjiang
					has_global_flag = NSG_no_mengjiang
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = NSG_yes_mengjiang
				}
				ECA = {
					country_event = {
						hours = 3 id = rcmjapan.94
					}
				}
				effect_tooltip = {
					ECA = {
						puppet = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = NSG_no_mengjiang
				}
				ECA = {
					country_event = {
						hours = 3 id = rcmjapan.96
					}
				}
				effect_tooltip = {
					ECA = {
						puppet = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			effect_tooltip = {
				ECA = {
					puppet = ROOT
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = SCG_no_mengjiang
		}
	}
	option = { #ONE YES
		name = rcmjapan.91.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				country_exists = NSG
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {

				target = NSG transfer_troops = yes
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = SCG transfer_troops = yes
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			JAP = {
				annex_country = {
				target = NSG transfer_troops = yes
				}
				annex_country = {
					target = SCG transfer_troops = yes
				}
			}
			clr_global_flag = scg_exists
			clr_global_flag = nsg_exists
			transfer_state = 1013
			transfer_state = 611
		}
		set_capital = { state = 611 }
	}
}

#NSG
country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.99
	title = rcmjapan.99.t
	desc = rcmjapan.99.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NSG
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		OR = {
			any_enemy_country = {
				is_legit_china = yes
			}
			event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {
				exists = no
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = mej_exists
				has_global_flag = nsg_no_puppet
				country_exists = NSG
			}
		}
		1013 = {
			is_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = yes
			#is_owned_by = JAP
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan.99.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = NSG_establish_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = nsg_exists
			NSG = {
				transfer_state = 1013
				add_state_core = 1013
			}
			JAP = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = NSG
					autonomous_state = autonomy_wtt_imperial_protectorate
				}
			}
			NSG = {
				set_politics = { ruling_party = fascism elections_allowed = no }
				set_political_party = { ideology = neutrality popularity = 35 }
				set_political_party = { ideology = fascism popularity = 65 }
				set_political_party = { ideology = communism popularity = 0 }
				set_political_party = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0 }
				set_political_party = { ideology = n_socialism popularity = 0 }
			}

		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "No need for that."
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = scg_no_puppet
		}
	}
}

#JAP CRUSH COM MILITIA
country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.105
	title = rcmjapan.105.t
	desc = rcmjapan.105.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_japan_army_mountainside
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			country_exists = PRC
		}
		OR = {
			is_subject_of = JAP
			tag = JAP
		}
		any_owned_state = {
			has_state_flag = commie_ridden_states
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan.105.a
		add_political_power = -100
		add_stability = 0.05
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				has_state_flag = commie_ridden_states
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = remove_com_par_act_tt
			clr_state_flag = commie_ridden_states
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = i_cracked_down_on_you

		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.106
	title = rcmjapan.106.t
	desc = rcmjapan.106.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_japan_army_mountainside
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan.106.a
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = MAN
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = MAN_JAP
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
				#create_country_leader = {
				#	name = "Zheng Xiaoxu"
				#	picture = "Portrait_MAN_Zheng_Xiaoxu.dds"
				#	expire = "1960.1.1"
				#	ideology = moderatism
				#	traits = {
				#		staunch_monarchist
				#	}
				#}
				retire_country_leader = yes
				zheng_xiaoxu = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							expire = "1965.1.1"
							ideology = moderatism
							traits = {
							}
						} 
					}
				}
				add_country_leader_trait = staunch_monarchist
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = ECA
				has_global_flag = ECA_MAF_exist

			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = ECA_MAF
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = mej_exists
				tag = ECA
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = MEJ
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				tag = ECA
				has_global_flag = mua_exists
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = MUA
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				tag = ECA
				has_global_flag = men_exists

			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = MEN
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SIK
			}
			kill_country_leader = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = XSM
				has_government = neutrality
			}			
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "XSM_ma_hongbin"
				desc = "POLITICS_MA_HONGBIN_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/NXM/Portrait_NXM_Ma_Hongbin.dds"
				expire = "1952.1.1"
				ideology = despotism
				traits = {
				}
			}
			
			set_cosmetic_tag = XSM_HUI
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = XSM
				has_government = n_socialism
			}			
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "XSM_ma_hongbin"
				desc = "POLITICS_MA_HONGBIN_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/NXM/Portrait_NXM_Ma_Hongbin.dds"
				expire = "1952.1.1"
				ideology = n_authoritarian_socialism
				traits = {
				}
			}			
			set_cosmetic_tag = XSM_HUI
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
				has_government = democratic
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Shen_Junru"
				desc = "POLITICS_Shen_Junru_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CHI/Portrait_CHI_Shen_Junru.dds"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = n_democratic_socialism
				traits = {
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_rrc = yes
				has_government = neutrality
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Chen_Gongbo"
				desc = "POLITICS_WANG_JINGWEI_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CHI/Portrait_CHI_Chen_Gongbo.dds"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = despotism
				traits = {
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_rrc = yes
				has_government = n_socialism
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Chen_Gongbo"
				desc = "POLITICS_WANG_JINGWEI_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CHI/Portrait_CHI_Chen_Gongbo.dds"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = n_authoritarian_socialism
				traits = {
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = {
						has_government = n_socialism
					}
				}
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 0.4
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				elections_allowed = no
			}

			FROM = {
				country_event = rcmjapan.1061
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = n_socialism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = n_socialism
				popularity = 0.4
			}
			FROM = {
				country_event = rcmjapan.1062
			}
		}
		add_ideas = reformed_colonial_administration
	}
}

					}

						array = GER.subjects

						}

	}

#OVERLORD
country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan.108
	title = wtt_japan.1.t
	desc = wtt_japan.1.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_japanese_transport_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Accept transfer puppet
	#Checking for puppet in decision that fires event.
	option = {
		name = wtt_japan.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = MAL
					tag = SST
					tag = FIC
					tag = INS
					tag = BOR
					tag = SAR	
				}
				is_puppet_of = ROOT
			}
			set_country_flag = Pacific_gaurdian_flag
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = FIC
				}
				release = CAM
				release = VIN
				release = LAO
				FROM = {
					puppet = CAM
					puppet = VIN
					puppet = LAO
				}
			}
			else = {
				FROM = {
					puppet = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = rcmjapan.109 days = 1 } }
	}

	#Refuse
	option = {
		name = wtt_japan.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = rcmjapan.110 days = 1 } }
	}
}

			base = 0
		}

			country_event = rcmjapan.113
		}
		set_global_flag = JAP_accepted_hull_note_demands
		add_ideas = free_trade
		white_peace = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_literally_china = yes
					is_subject_of = HOL
					is_subject_of = ENG

				}
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = USA
				}
				NOT = {
					OVERLORD = {
						has_war_with = USA
					}
				}
			}

				white_peace = PREV
			}
		}

			limit = {
				NOT = {
					USA = {

					}
				}
			}

			}
			if = {
				limit = {

					}
				}

			}

			    relation = non_aggression_pact
			    active = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					USA = {
						has_war_with = HOL
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					JAP = {
						has_war_with = HOL
					}
				}
				white_peace = HOL
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
			    country = HOL
			    relation = non_aggression_pact
			    active = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {

					}
				}
			}

#Canton Operation - JAP
country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan_canton.121
	title = rcmjapan_canton.121.t
	desc = rcmjapan_canton.121.d

    trigger = {
		is_ai = yes
		original_tag = JAP
		surrender_progress < 0.01
		608 = {
			is_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = yes
		}
		716 = {
			is_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = yes
		}
		328 = {
			is_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = yes
		}
		any_enemy_country = {
			owns_state = 592
		}
		592 = {
			is_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = no
		}
		date > 1938.10.1
		date < 1940.1.1
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_japanese_transport_soldiers
	
	is_triggered_only = no
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		
		#set_global_flag = JAP_battle_of_shanghai_happened
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { controls_state = 592 }}
				592 = {
					owner = {
                        country_event = { id = rcmjapan_canton.122 hours = 1 }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_template = "Hohei Shidan"
						}
					}

country_event = { #Motion of no confidence
	id = rcmjapan.122
	title = rcmjapan.122.t
	desc = rcmjapan.122.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_public_hearing_2
	#immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rcmjapan.1"}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan.122.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				#always = yes
				has_country_flag = RCM_unrest_against_yonai_flag
			}
			clear_all_cabinet_members_JAP = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = blank_line
			drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
			unlock_national_focus = JAP_second_konoe_cabinet_focus
			custom_effect_tooltip = blank_line
			country_event = rcmjapan_pm.9
			add_popularity = {
			    ideology = fascism
			    popularity = 0.4
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = fascism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = fascism
				name = JAP_fascism_party_tai
				long_name = JAP_fascism_party_tai
			}
			add_ideas = new_order
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = JAP_military_outweighs_the_government_idea_bad
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					add_idea = JAP_military_outweighs_the_government_idea_good
					remove_idea = JAP_military_outweighs_the_government_idea_bad
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = JAP_military_outweighs_the_government_idea
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					add_idea = JAP_military_outweighs_the_government_idea_good
					remove_idea = JAP_military_outweighs_the_government_idea
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "Waking the Tiger"
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = JAP_interservice_rivalry_navy_dominant
					add_idea = JAP_interservice_rivalry_army_dominant
				}
			}			
			clr_country_flag = RCM_unrest_against_yonai_flag
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RCM_pro_axis_unrest_YONAI_flag
			}
			clear_all_cabinet_members_JAP = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = blank_line
			drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
			unlock_national_focus = JAP_second_konoe_cabinet_focus
			custom_effect_tooltip = blank_line
			country_event = rcmjapan_pm.9
			add_popularity = {
			    ideology = fascism
			    popularity = 0.4
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = fascism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = fascism
				name = JAP_fascism_party_tai
				long_name = JAP_fascism_party_tai
			}
			add_ideas = new_order
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = JAP_military_outweighs_the_government_idea_bad
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					add_idea = JAP_military_outweighs_the_government_idea_good
					remove_idea = JAP_military_outweighs_the_government_idea_bad
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = JAP_military_outweighs_the_government_idea
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					add_idea = JAP_military_outweighs_the_government_idea_good
					remove_idea = JAP_military_outweighs_the_government_idea
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "Waking the Tiger"
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = JAP_interservice_rivalry_navy_dominant
					add_idea = JAP_interservice_rivalry_army_dominant
				}
			}	
			clr_country_flag = RCM_pro_axis_unrest_YONAI_flag
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RCM_pro_axis_unrest_KONOE_flag
			}
			clear_all_cabinet_members_JAP = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = blank_line
			if = {
				limit = {
					sign_triparti_pact_bypass_trigger = yes
				}
				random_country = {
					limit = {
						owns_state = 988
						OR = {
							is_in_faction_with = GER
							is_subject_of = GER
							AND = {
								original_tag = FRA
								has_government = fascism
							}
						}
					}
					country_event = {

						days = 1
					}
				}

				custom_effect_tooltip = blank_line
			}

country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan_expand_revo.40
	title = rcmjapan_expand_revo.40.t
	desc = rcmjapan_expand_revo.40.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_riot
	trigger = {
		JAP = {
			has_government = communism
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = JAP_subversion_flag
				is_puppet = no
				communism > 0.5
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = JAP_subversion_flag
				is_puppet = yes
				communism > 0.75
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_expand_revo.40.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = SST 
				num_of_controlled_states < 1
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = submit_oof
		JAP = { country_event = { id = rcmjapan_expand_revo.41 days = 1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_expand_revo.40.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = SST 
			}
			num_of_controlled_states > 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_puppet = yes
			}
			OVERLORD = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_war_with = FROM
						}
					}
					set_country_flag = peace_on_war_ends_flag
					FROM = {
						set_country_flag = peace_on_war_ends_flag
					}
				}
			}
		}
		start_civil_war = {
			ideology = communism
			size = 0.5
		}
		JAP = { country_event = { id = rcmjapan_expand_revo.41 days = 1 } }
	}
}

country_event = {

	desc = rcmjapan_althist.2.d

		hidden_effect = {
			scoped_sound_effect = gun_shot_sound
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_althist.2.a
		
		hidden_effect = {
			
			613 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
				set_global_flag = no_shanghai_DMZ
			}
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
			type = annex_everything
		}
		event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {
			kill_country_leader = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = democratic_start_cw_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				start_civil_war = {
					ideology = democratic
					size = 0.3
					###only_own_territory = yes
					capital = 613
					states = {
						613
					}
					keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { always = yes }
				}
			}

			random_enemy_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = CPG
				load_focus_tree = warlord_generic_nationalist
				save_global_event_target_as = CDL_JAP_puppet
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = {
							has_war_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
						}
					}
					event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {
						PREV = {
							add_to_war = {
								targeted_alliance = JAP
								enemy = PREV
							}
						}
					}
				}

				JAP = {
					add_to_faction = PREV
				}
				for_each_scope_loop = {
					array = WTT_current_china_leader.core_states
					THIS = {
						add_core_of = event_target:CDL_JAP_puppet
					}
				}
				get_current_government_type = yes
				JAP = {
					puppet = event_target:CDL_JAP_puppet
				}
				restore_previous_government_type = yes
				create_country_leader = {
					name = Zhang_Lan
					desc = "POLITICS_ZHANG_LAN_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_China_Zhang_Lan.dds"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = socialism
					traits = {
						#
					}
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = shanghai_will_be_CDL
	}
}

country_event = {

	desc = rcmjapan_althist.10.d

	#hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	#is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_strengthen_civilian_government }
		focus_progress = {
			focus = JAP_strengthen_civilian_government
			progress > 0.3
		}
		has_idea = JAP_peace_preservation_law
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_althist.10.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 
				OR = {					
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = JAP_ai_behavior
						option = OKADA_STAYS_STATE_SOCIALISM
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = JAP_ai_behavior
						option = OKADA_STAYS_COMMUNISM
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = JAP_ai_behavior
						option = OKADA_STAYS_TOHOKAI
					}
				}
			}			
		}		
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = JAP_peace_preservation_law
			add_idea = JAP_peace_preservation_law_better
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = allow_treaty_faction_branch_tt
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_althist.10.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = JAP_ai_behavior
					option = OKADA_STAYS_TREATY_FACTION
				}
			}			
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = JAP_peace_preservation_law
				add_idea = JAP_no_peace_preservation_law
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = JAP_peace_preservation_law
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = allow_socialist_branch_tt
	}
}

					size > 4

				}
			}
		}

		}

add_namespace = rcmjapan_christian_ban_persecution_backlash
#996 Tokachi backlash
country_event = { 
	id = rcmjapan_christian_ban_persecution_backlash.1
	title = rcmjapan_christian_ban_persecution_backlash.1.t
	desc = rcmjapan_christian_ban_persecution_backlash.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_asian_unrest_2
	#immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rcmjapan_althist.2"}
	#fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		JAP = {
			set_country_flag = crack_down_in_process_christian
		}
		996 = {
			set_state_flag = This_state_has_backlash
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_christian_ban_persecution_backlash.1.a
		trigger = {
			always = no #this cause bugs, player can use decision later
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = Back_lash_active
		996 = {
			save_global_event_target_as = pacify_christian_state
		}
		JAP = {			
			clr_country_flag = crack_down_in_process_christian
			activate_mission = RCM_send_in_the_garrison_mission
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_christian_ban_persecution_backlash.1.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = Back_lash_active
		JAP = {			
			clr_country_flag = crack_down_in_process_christian
		}
	}
}

add_namespace = rcmjapan_christian_constitutionalize_religious_freedom_backlash
#996 Tokachi backlash
country_event = { 
	id = rcmjapan_christian_constitutionalize_religious_freedom_backlash.1
	title = rcmjapan_christian_constitutionalize_religious_freedom_backlash.1.t
	desc = rcmjapan_christian_constitutionalize_religious_freedom_backlash.1.d
	picture = report_event_asian_unrest_2
	#immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rcmjapan_althist.2"}
	#fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		JAP = {
			set_country_flag = crack_down_in_process_christian
		}
		996 = {
			set_state_flag = This_state_has_backlash
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_christian_constitutionalize_religious_freedom_backlash.1.a
		trigger = {
			always = no #this cause bugs, player can use decision later
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = Back_lash_active
		996 = {
			save_global_event_target_as = pacify_christian_state
		}
		JAP = {			
			clr_country_flag = crack_down_in_process_christian
			activate_mission = RCM_send_in_the_garrison_mission
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_christian_constitutionalize_religious_freedom_backlash.1.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = Back_lash_active
		JAP = {			
			clr_country_flag = crack_down_in_process_christian
		}
	}
}

	id = rcmjapan_christian_constitutionalize_religious_freedom_backlash.6
	title = rcmjapan_christian_constitutionalize_religious_freedom_backlash.6.t
	desc = rcmjapan_christian_constitutionalize_religious_freedom_backlash.6.d
	picture = report_event_asian_unrest_2
	#immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rcmjapan_althist.2"}
	#fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		JAP = {
			set_country_flag = crack_down_in_process_christian
		}
		282 = {
			set_state_flag = This_state_has_backlash
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_christian_constitutionalize_religious_freedom_backlash.6.a
		trigger = {
			always = no #this cause bugs, player can use decision later
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = Back_lash_active
		282 = {
			save_global_event_target_as = pacify_christian_state
		}
		JAP = {			
			clr_country_flag = crack_down_in_process_christian
			activate_mission = RCM_send_in_the_garrison_mission
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_christian_constitutionalize_religious_freedom_backlash.6.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = Back_lash_active
		JAP = {			
			clr_country_flag = crack_down_in_process_christian
		}
	}
}

add_namespace = rcmjapan_baseball_news
#season start news
news_event = {
	id = rcmjapan_baseball_news.1
	title = rcmjapan_baseball_news.1.t
	desc = rcmjapan_baseball_news.1.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_baseball_opening
	#immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rcmjapan_althist.2"}
	#fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			ROOT = {
				sound_effect = baseball_1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = stake_level_1 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = stake_level_2 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = stake_level_3 }
			}
			set_country_flag = stake_level_1
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_baseball_news.1.a		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = opt_out_of_baseball_bets }
			}
			country_event = rcmjapan_baseball.1
		}
	}
}
#season end news
news_event = {
	id = rcmjapan_baseball_news.2
	title = rcmjapan_baseball_news.2.t
	desc = rcmjapan_baseball_news.2.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_baseball_ending
	#immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rcmjapan_althist.2"}
	#fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_baseball_news.2.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = I_won_this_match_champion
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = autorun_on
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_baseball_news.2.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = I_won_this_match_champion
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_baseball_news.2.c
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = autorun_on
		}
	}
}
add_namespace = rcmjapan_baseball
#first intro event
country_event = {
	id = rcmjapan_baseball.1
	title = rcmjapan_baseball.1.t
	desc = rcmjapan_baseball.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_stadium
	#immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rcmjapan_althist.2"}
	#fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		clr_baseball_game_data = yes
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = opt_out_of_baseball_bets
		}
	}
	option = { #intro
		name = rcmjapan_baseball.1.a
		country_event = rcmjapan_baseball.2	
	}
	option = { #skip to choosing
		name = rcmjapan_baseball.1.b
		country_event = rcmjapan_baseball.8	
	}
	option = { #opt out of bets
		name = rcmjapan_baseball.1.c
		custom_effect_tooltip = opt_out_of_baseball_bets_tt
		set_country_flag = opt_out_of_baseball_bets
		set_country_flag = autorun_on
		activate_mission = RCM_JAP_game_in_progress_no_champion_mission
	}
}

#choose event
country_event = { 
	id = rcmjapan_baseball.8
	title = rcmjapan_baseball.8.t
	desc = rcmjapan_baseball.8.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_baseball
	#immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rcmjapan_althist.8"}
	#fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	#Hosei
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_baseball.8.a
		set_country_flag = I_chose_hosei
		start_baseball_game = yes
	}
	#Keio
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_baseball.8.b
		set_country_flag = I_chose_keio
		start_baseball_game = yes
	}
	#Rikkyo
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_baseball.8.c
		set_country_flag = I_chose_rikkyo
		start_baseball_game = yes
	}
	#Waseda(not expanded)
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_baseball.8.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_completed_focus = JAP_expand_the_Tokyo_Big6_Baseball_League_focus
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = I_chose_waseda
		start_baseball_game = yes
	}
	#next page
	option = { 
		name = rcmjapan_baseball.8.e
		trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = JAP_expand_the_Tokyo_Big6_Baseball_League_focus
		}
		country_event = rcmjapan_baseball.81
	}
	
}
#choose page 2nd
country_event = { 
	id = rcmjapan_baseball.81
	title = rcmjapan_baseball.81.t
	desc = rcmjapan_baseball.81.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_baseball
	#immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rcmjapan_althist.8"}
	#fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	#Waseda
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_baseball.8.a
		set_country_flag = I_chose_waseda
		start_baseball_game = yes
	}
	#Meiji
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_baseball.8.b
		set_country_flag = I_chose_meiji
		start_baseball_game = yes
	}
	#Tokyo
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_baseball.8.c
		set_country_flag = I_chose_tokyo
		start_baseball_game = yes
	}
	# last page
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_baseball.8.d
		country_event = rcmjapan_baseball.8
	}
	
}

#announcement when events finished

#won champion
country_event = { 
	id = rcmjapan_baseball.9
	title = rcmjapan_baseball.9.t
	desc = rcmjapan_baseball.9.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_baseball_victory
	#immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rcmjapan_althist.2"}
	#fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_baseball.9.a
		add_political_power = This.reward_pp
		add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = This.reward_civ }
	}
}

	#immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rcmjapan_althist.2"}
	#fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_baseball.10.a
		add_political_power = This.reward_pp
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = civies_finished_last_low_stake
			}
			remove_a_random_civ = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = civies_finished_last_mid_stake
			}
			remove_a_random_civ = yes
			remove_a_random_civ = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = civies_finished_last_high_stake
			}
			remove_a_random_civ = yes
			remove_a_random_civ = yes
			remove_a_random_civ = yes
		}
		else = {
			add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = This.reward_civ }
		}
	}
}

			JAP = {
				scoped_sound_effect = drum_02
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmjapan_left_reform.1.a
		trigger = {
			has_dlc = "Waking the Tiger"
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 200
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = JAP_ai_behavior 
					option = OKADA_STAYS_COMMUNISM
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = rcmjapan_left_reform_a_tt
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = 0.08
		}
		add_manpower = 5000
		MAN = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = n_socialism
				popularity = -0.03
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = -0.03
			}
			add_manpower = -5000
			country_event = rcmjapan_left_reform.2
			remove_ideas = strikes_1
			clr_country_flag = crisis_in_progress
		}
	}

			clr_country_flag = crisis_in_progress
		}
	}

			base = 1
			modifier = {
